<li id="cite_note-annexed-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-annexed_1-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Including de facto <a href="/wiki/Areas_annexed_by_Nazi_Germany" title="Areas annexed by Nazi Germany">annexed/incorporated territories</a>.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-vacant-2"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-vacant_2-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The office formally became vacant on Hitler's death. His titles were <a href="/wiki/F%C3%BChrer_und_Reichskanzler" class="mw-redirect" title="Führer und Reichskanzler">Führer und Reichskanzler</a> from August 1934. See <a href="#CITEREFGesetz_.C3.BCber_das_Staatsoberhaupt1934">Gesetz über das Staatsoberhaupt 1934</a>.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-statistics-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-statistics_3-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">In 1939, before Germany acquired control of the last two regions which had been in its control before the Versailles Treaty—Alsace-Lorraine, Danzig, and the Polish Corridor—its area was 633,786 square kilometres (244,706&#160;sq&#160;mi). See <a href="#CITEREFStatistisches_Jahrbuch2006">Statistisches Jahrbuch 2006</a>.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-4">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation journal">"Die Bevölkerung des Deutschen Reichs nach den Ergebnissen der Volkszählung 1939, Berlin 1941." (2).</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ANazi+Germany&amp;rft.atitle=Die+Bev%C3%B6lkerung+des+Deutschen+Reichs+nach+den+Ergebnissen+der+Volksz%C3%A4hlung+1939%2C+Berlin+1941.&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.issue=2&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal" class="Z3988"><span style="display:none;">&#160;</span></span></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-abbreviation-8"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-abbreviation_8-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The party's name in German was <i>Nationalsozialistische Deutsche Arbeiterpartei</i>.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-estimate-144"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-estimate_144-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">On 29 November 2006 State Secretary in the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Ministry_of_the_Interior_(Germany)" title="Federal Ministry of the Interior (Germany)">Federal Ministry of the Interior</a> <a href="/wiki/Christoph_Bergner" title="Christoph Bergner">Christoph Bergner</a> said the reason the statistics do not match is because Haar only includes people who were directly killed. The figure of 2 to 2.5 million also includes people who died of disease, hunger, cold, air raids, and other causes. <a href="#CITEREFKoldehoff2006">Koldehoff 2006</a>. The <a href="/wiki/German_Red_Cross" title="German Red Cross">German Red Cross</a> still maintains that the death toll from the expulsions is 2.2 million. <a href="#CITEREFKammererKammerer2005">Kammerer &amp; Kammerer 2005</a>, p.&#160;12.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-districts-154"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-districts_154-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">More such districts, such as the <i><a href="/wiki/Reichskommissariat_Moskowien" title="Reichskommissariat Moskowien">Reichskommissariat Moskowien</a></i> (Moscow), <i><a href="/wiki/Reichskommissariat_Kaukasus" title="Reichskommissariat Kaukasus">Reichskommissariat Kaukasus</a></i> (Caucasus), and <i><a href="/wiki/Reichskommissariat_Turkestan" title="Reichskommissariat Turkestan">Reichskommissariat Turkestan</a></i> (Turkestan) were proposed in the event that these areas were brought under German rule.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-quote-300"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-quote_300-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">"Nevertheless, the available evidence suggests that, on the whole, ordinary Germans did not approve. Goebbel's propaganda campaigns carried out in the second half of 1941 and again in 1943 had failed to convert them." <a href="#CITEREFEvans2008">Evans 2008</a>, p.&#160;561.</span></li>
</ol>
